# <a name="search-the-audit-log-in-the-security--compliance-center"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-103">在安全 & 合规性中心中搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-103">Search the audit log in the Security & Compliance Center</span></span>

## <a name="introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-104">简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-104">Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-105">需要查找用户是否查看了特定文档或清除了其邮箱中的项目？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-105">Need to find if a user viewed a specific document or purged an item from their mailbox?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-106">如果是这样, 您可以使用 Office 365 安全&amp;合规中心搜索统一审核日志, 以查看 Office 365 组织中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-106">If so, you can use the Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center to search the unified audit log to view user and administrator activity in your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-107">为什么要使用统一审核日志？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-107">Why a unified audit log?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-108">由于您可以在 Office 365 中搜索以下类型的用户和管理员活动:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-108">Because you can search for the following types of user and admin activity in Office 365:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-109">SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for business 中的用户活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-109">User activity in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-110">Exchange Online 中的用户活动 (Exchange 邮箱审核日志记录)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-110">User activity in Exchange Online (Exchange mailbox audit logging)</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-111">SharePoint Online 中的管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-111">Admin activity in SharePoint Online</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-112">Azure Active Directory 中的管理活动 (Office 365 的目录服务)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-112">Admin activity in Azure Active Directory (the directory service for Office 365)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-113">Exchange Online 中的管理员活动 (Exchange 管理员审核日志记录)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-113">Admin activity in Exchange Online (Exchange admin audit logging)</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-114">Sway 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-114">User and admin activity in Sway</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-115">安全与合规中心中的电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-115">eDiscovery activities in the security and compliance center</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-116">Power BI 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-116">User and admin activity in Power BI</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-117">Microsoft 团队中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-117">User and admin activity in Microsoft Teams</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-118">Dynamics 365 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-118">User and admin activity in Dynamics 365</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-119">Yammer 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-119">User and admin activity in Yammer</span></span>
 
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-120">Microsoft Flow 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-120">User and admin activity in Microsoft Flow</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-121">Microsoft Stream 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-121">User and admin activity in Microsoft Stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-122">Microsoft 工作区分析中的分析师和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-122">Analyst and admin activity in Microsoft Workplace Analytics</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-123">Microsoft PowerApps 中的用户和管理员活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-123">User and admin activity in Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>
    
   
## <a name="before-you-begin"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-124">开始之前</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-124">Before you begin</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-125">在开始搜索 Office 365 审核日志之前, 请务必阅读以下各项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-125">Be sure to read the following items before you start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-126">您 (或另一个管理员) 必须先启用审核日志记录, 然后才能开始搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-126">You (or another admin) must first turn on audit logging before you can start searching the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-127">若要打开它, 只需单击安全性 & 合规性中心中的 "**审核日志搜索**" 页上的 "**开始记录用户和管理员活动**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-127">To turn it on, just click **Start recording user and admin activity** on the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-128">(如果看不到此链接, 表明已为您的组织启用了审核。)打开后, 会显示一条消息, 指出正在准备审核日志, 并且您可以在准备完成后的几小时内运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-128">(If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.) After you turn it on, a message is displayed that says the audit log is being prepared and that you can run a search in a couple of hours after the preparation is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-129">您只需执行一次此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-129">You only have to do this once.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="81889-130">默认情况下, 我们正在启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-130">We're in the process of turning on auditing by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-131">在此之前, 你可以按照前面所述将其打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-131">Until then, you can turn it on as previously described.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-132">您必须在 Exchange Online 中向您分配 "仅查看审核日志" 或 "审核日志" 角色, 才能搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-132">You have to be assigned the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role in Exchange Online to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-133">默认情况下, 将这些角色分配给 Exchange 管理中心中 "**权限**" 页上的 "合规性管理" 和 "组织管理" 角色组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-133">By default, these roles are assigned to the Compliance Management and Organization Management role groups on the **Permissions** page in the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-134">请注意, Office 365 和 Microsoft 365 中的全局管理员将自动添加为 Exchange Online 中的 "组织管理" 角色组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-134">Note that global administrators in Office 365 and Microsoft 365 are automatically added as members of the Organization Management role group in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-135">若要使用户能够使用最低级别的权限搜索 Office 365 审核日志, 您可以在 Exchange Online 中创建自定义角色组, 添加仅查看审核日志或审核日志角色, 然后将该用户添加为新角色组的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-135">To give a user the ability to search the Office 365 audit log with the minimum level of privileges, you can create a custom role group in Exchange Online, add the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role, and then add the user as a member of the new role group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-136">有关详细信息, 请参阅[在 Exchange Online 中管理角色组](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-136">For more information, see [Manage role groups in Exchange Online](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=730688).</span></span>
    
    > [!IMPORTANT]
    > <span data-ttu-id="81889-137">如果在 Security & 合规性中心中向用户分配 "**权限**" 页上的 "仅查看" "审核日志" 或 "审核日志" 角色, 则他们将无法搜索 Office 365 审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-137">If you assign a user the View-Only Audit Logs or Audit Logs role on the **Permissions** page in the Security & Compliance Center, they won't be able to search the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-138">您必须在 Exchange Online 中分配权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-138">You have to assign the permissions in Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-139">这是因为用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是 Exchange Online cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-139">This is because the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-140">当用户或管理员执行了审核的活动时, 将生成审核记录并将其存储在组织的 Office 365 审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-140">When an audited activity is performed by a user or admin, an audit record is generated and stored in the Office 365 audit log for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-141">审核记录保留的时间长度 (并可在审核日志中搜索) 取决于您的 Office 365 订阅, 以及分配给特定用户的许可证类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-141">The length of time that an audit record is retained (and searchable in the audit log) depends on your Office 365 subscription, and specifically the type of the license that is assigned to a specific user.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="81889-142">**Office 365 E3** -审核记录保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-142">**Office 365 E3** - Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-143">这意味着, 您可以在审核日志中搜索在过去的90天内执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-143">That means you can search the audit log for activities that were performed within the last 90 days.</span></span>

     - <span data-ttu-id="81889-144">**Office 365 E5** -审核记录也会保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-144">**Office 365 E5** - Audit records are also retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-145">保留一年的审核记录可能最终适用于拥有 E3 许可证和 Office 365 高级合规性附加许可证的 E5 用户和用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-145">Retaining audit records for one year may eventually be available for E5 users and users with an E3 license and an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on license.</span></span>

        > [!NOTE]
        > <span data-ttu-id="81889-146">用于 E5 组织 (或具有高级合规性附加许可证的 E3 组织中的用户) 的审核记录的为期一年保留期的专用预览计划将关闭到新的注册。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-146">The private preview program for the one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or for users in E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is closed to new enrollment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-147">此文章将在公开预览版中的一年保留期可用或发布以用于正式可用性时进行更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-147">This article will be updated when the one-year retention period is available in public preview or released for general availability.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-148">如果要关闭组织的 Office 365 中的审核日志搜索, 可以在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行以下命令:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-148">If you want to turn off audit log search in Office 365 for your organization, you can run the following command in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $false
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="81889-149">若要再次启用审核搜索, 您可以在 Exchange Online PowerShell 中运行以下命令:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-149">To turn on audit search again, you can run the following command in Exchange Online PowerShell:</span></span>
    
  ```
  Set-AdminAuditLogConfig -UnifiedAuditLogIngestionEnabled $true
  ```

    <span data-ttu-id="81889-150">有关详细信息, 请参阅[在 Office 365 中关闭审核日志搜索](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-150">For more information, see [Turn off audit log search in Office 365](turn-audit-log-search-on-or-off.md).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-151">如前面所述, 用于搜索审核日志的基础 cmdlet 是**UnifiedAuditLog**的 Exchange Online cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-151">As previously stated, the underlying cmdlet used to search the audit log is an Exchange Online cmdlet, which is **Search-UnifiedAuditLog**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-152">这意味着您可以使用此 cmdlet 搜索 Office 365 审核日志, 而不是使用安全 & 合规性中心中的 "**审核日志搜索**" 页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-152">That means you can use this cmdlet to search the Office 365 audit log instead of using the **Audit log search** page in the Security & Compliance Center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-153">您必须在连接到 Exchange Online 组织的远程 PowerShell 中运行此 cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-153">You have to run this cmdlet in remote PowerShell connected to your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-154">有关详细信息, 请参阅[UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-154">For more information, see [Search-UnifiedAuditLog](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=834776).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-155">如果要以编程方式从 Office 365 审核日志中下载数据, 我们建议使用 Office 365 管理活动 API, 而不是使用 PowerShell 脚本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-155">If you want to programmatically download data from the Office 365 audit log, we recommend that you use the Office 365 Management Activity API instead of using a PowerShell script.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-156">Office 365 管理活动 API 是 REST web 服务, 可用于为组织开发操作、安全性和合规性监视解决方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-156">The Office 365 Management Activity API is a REST web service that you can use to develop operations, security, and compliance monitoring solutions for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-157">有关详细信息, 请参阅[Office 365 管理活动 API 参考](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-157">For more information, see [Office 365 Management Activity API reference](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/office-365-management-activity-api-reference).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-158">在事件发生后, 将在搜索结果中显示相应的审核日志条目, 最长可能需要30分钟或最长24小时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-158">It can take up to 30 minutes or up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-159">下表显示了 Office 365 中的不同服务所需的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-159">The following table shows the time it takes for the different services in Office 365.</span></span>
    
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-160">**Office 365 服务**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-160">**Office 365 service**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-161">**30 分钟**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-161">**30 minutes**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-162">**24 小时制**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-162">**24 hours**</span></span>|
    |:-----|:-----|:-----|
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-163">高级威胁防护和威胁智能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-163">Advanced Threat Protection and Threat Intelligence</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)| |
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-165">Azure Active Directory (用户登录事件)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-165">Azure Active Directory (user login events)</span></span>  <br/> ||![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |

    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-189">SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-189">SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business</span></span>  <br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> ||
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-191">Sway</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-191">Sway</span></span>  <br/> ||![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-193">工作区分析</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-193">Workplace Analytics</span></span><br/> |![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> || 
    |<span data-ttu-id="81889-195">Yammer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-195">Yammer</span></span>  <br/> ||![复选标记](media/f3b4c351-17d9-42d9-8540-e48e01779b31.png)           <br/> |
   
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-197">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 是 Office 365 的目录服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-197">Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) is the directory service for Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-198">统一审核日志包含在 Microsoft 365 管理中心或在 Azure 管理门户中执行的用户、组、应用程序、域和目录活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-198">The unified audit log contains user, group, application, domain, and directory activities performed in the Microsoft 365 admin center or in the in Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-199">有关 Azure AD 事件的完整列表, 请参阅[Azure Active Directory 审核报告事件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-199">For a complete list of Azure AD events, see [Azure Active Directory Audit Report Events](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=616549).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-200">Exchange Online 审核日志包含两种类型的事件: Exchange 管理员事件 (由管理员执行的操作) 和邮箱事件 (由用户对邮箱执行的操作)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-200">Exchange Online audit logs consist of two types of events: Exchange admin events (actions taken by administrators) and mailbox events (actions taken by users on mailboxes).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-201">请注意, 默认情况下不启用邮箱审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-201">Note that mailbox auditing isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-202">必须为每个用户邮箱启用邮箱事件, 然后才能在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索邮箱事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-202">It must be enable for each user mailbox before mailbox events can be searched for in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-203">有关邮箱审核和所记录的邮箱审核操作的详细信息, 请参阅[在 Office 365 中启用邮箱审核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-203">For more information about mailbox auditing and the mailbox auditing actions that are logged, see [Enable mailbox auditing in Office 365](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-204">Power BI 的审核日志记录默认情况下不启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-204">Audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-205">若要在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动, 您必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-205">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-206">有关说明, 请参阅[POWER BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的 "审核日志" 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-206">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>
    
    
## <a name="search-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-207">搜索审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-207">Search the audit log</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-208">以下是在 Office 365 中搜索审核日志的过程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-208">Here's the process for searching the audit log in Office 365.</span></span>
  
[<span data-ttu-id="81889-209">步骤 1: 运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-209">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>](#step-1-run-an-audit-log-search)
  
[<span data-ttu-id="81889-210">步骤 2: 查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-210">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>](#step-2-view-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="81889-211">步骤 3: 筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-211">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)

[<span data-ttu-id="81889-212">步骤 4: 将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-212">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>](#step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file)
  
### <a name="step-1-run-an-audit-log-search"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-213">步骤 1: 运行审核日志搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-213">Step 1: Run an audit log search</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="81889-214">转到 [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-214">Go to [https://protection.office.com](https://protection.office.com).</span></span>
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="81889-215">使用专用浏览会话 (而非常规会话) 访问安全 & 合规性中心, 因为这将阻止当前登录的凭据正在使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-215">Use a private browsing session (not a regular session) to access the Security & Compliance Center because this will prevent the credential that you are currently logged on with from being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-216">若要在 Internet Explorer 或 Microsoft Edge 中打开 InPrivate 浏览会话, 只需按 CTRL + SHIFT + P。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-216">To open an InPrivate Browsing session in Internet Explorer or Microsoft Edge, just press CTRL+SHIFT+P.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-217">若要在 Google Chrome 中打开一个专用浏览会话 (称为 incognito 窗口), 请按 CTRL + SHIFT + N。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-217">To open a private browsing session in Google Chrome (called an incognito window), press CTRL+SHIFT+N.</span></span> 
  
2. <span data-ttu-id="81889-218">使用工作或学校帐户登录到 Office 365。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-218">Sign in to Office 365 using your work or school account.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="81889-219">在安全性 & 合规性中心的左侧窗格中, 单击 "**搜索**", 然后单击 "**审核日志搜索**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-219">In the left pane of the Security & Compliance Center, click **Search**, and then click **Audit log search**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-220">将显示 "**审核日志搜索**" 页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-220">The **Audit log search** page is displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![配置条件, 然后单击 "搜索" 以运行报告](media/8639d09c-2843-44e4-8b4b-9f45974ff7f1.png)
  
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="81889-222">您必须先启用审核日志记录, 然后才能运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-222">You have to first turn on audit logging before you can run an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-223">如果显示 "**开始记录用户和管理员活动**" 链接, 请单击它以启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-223">If the **Start recording user and admin activity** link is displayed, click it to turn on auditing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-224">如果您看不到此链接, 表明已为您的组织启用了审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-224">If you don't see this link, auditing has already been turned on for your organization.</span></span> 
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="81889-225">配置以下搜索条件:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-225">Configure the following search criteria:</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-226">a.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-226">a.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-227">**活动**单击下拉列表以显示您可以搜索的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-227">**Activities** Click the drop-down list to display the activities that you can search for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-228">用户和管理员活动组织到相关活动的组中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-228">User and admin activities are organized in to groups of related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-229">您可以选择特定的活动, 也可以单击活动组名称以选择组中的所有活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-229">You can select specific activities or you can click the activity group name to select all activities in the group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-230">您还可以单击所选活动以清除所选内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-230">You can also click a selected activity to clear the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-231">运行搜索后, 仅显示所选活动的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-231">After you run the search, only the audit log entries for the selected activities are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-232">选择 "**显示所有活动的结果**" 将显示所选用户或用户组执行的所有活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-232">Selecting **Show results for all activities** will display results for all activities performed by the selected user or group of users.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-233">100以上的用户和管理员活动记录在 Office 365 审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-233">Over 100 user and admin activities are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-234">单击本文主题中的 "已**审核的活动**" 选项卡, 查看每个不同的 Office 365 服务中的每个活动的说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-234">Click the **Audited activities** tab at the topic of this article to see the descriptions of every activity in each of the different Office 365 services.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-235">b.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-235">b.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-236">默认情况下, 将选择 "**开始日期**" 和 "**结束日期**" 最后七天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-236">**Start date** and **End date** The last seven days are selected by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-237">选择要显示在该时间段内发生的事件的日期和时间范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-237">Select a date and time range to display the events that occurred within that period.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-238">日期和时间以协调通用时间 (UTC) 格式显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-238">The date and time are presented in Coordinated Universal Time (UTC) format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-239">您可以指定的最大日期范围为90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-239">The maximum date range that you can specify is 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-240">如果所选日期范围大于90天, 则显示错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-240">An error is displayed if the selected date range is greater than 90 days.</span></span> 
    
    > [!TIP]
    > <span data-ttu-id="81889-241">如果使用的最大日期范围是90天, 请选择 "**开始日期**" 的当前时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-241">If you're using the maximum date range of 90 days, select the current time for the **Start date**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-242">否则, 您将收到一条错误消息, 指出开始日期早于结束日期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-242">Otherwise, you'll receive an error saying that the start date is earlier than the end date.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-243">如果您在最近90天内启用了审核, 则在启用审核的日期之前, 最大日期范围无法开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-243">If you've turned on auditing within the last 90 days, the maximum date range can't start before the date that auditing was turned on.</span></span> 
  
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-244">c.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-244">c.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-245">**用户**在此框中单击, 然后选择要为其显示搜索结果的一个或多个用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-245">**Users** Click in this box and then select one or more users to display search results for.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-246">您在此框中选择的用户执行的选定活动的审核日志条目将显示在结果列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-246">The audit log entries for the selected activity performed by the users you select in this box are displayed in the list of results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-247">将此框保留为空将返回组织中所有用户 (和服务帐户) 的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-247">Leave this box blank to return entries for all users (and service accounts) in your organization.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-248">d.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-248">d.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-249">**文件、文件夹或网站**键入文件或文件夹名称的部分或全部, 以搜索与包含指定关键字的文件夹文件相关的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-249">**File, folder, or site** Type some or all of a file or folder name to search for activity related to the file of folder that contains the specified keyword.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-250">您还可以指定文件或文件夹的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-250">You can also specify a URL of a file or folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-251">如果使用 URL, 请确保键入完整的 URL 路径, 或者如果只键入 URL 的一部分, 则不要包含任何特殊字符或空格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-251">If you use a URL, be sure the type the full URL path or if you just type a portion of the URL, don't include any special characters or spaces.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-252">将此框保留为空将返回组织中的所有文件和文件夹的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-252">Leave this box blank to return entries for all files and folders in your organization.</span></span>
    
   <span data-ttu-id="81889-253">**几点**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-253">**TIPS**</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="81889-254">如果要查找与**网站**相关的所有活动, 请在 URL 后面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该网站的所有条目;例如, **https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/"\*"**。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-254">If you're looking for all activities related to a **site**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) after the URL to return all entries for that site; for example, **"https://contoso-my.sharepoint.com/personal/\*"**.</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="81889-255">如果要查找与**文件**相关的所有活动, 请在文件名前面添加通配符 (\*) 以返回该文件的所有条目;例如, \**"* Customer_Profitability_Sample"\*\*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-255">If you're looking for all activities related to a **file**, add the wildcard symbol (\*) before the file name to return all entries for that file; for example, **"\*Customer_Profitability_Sample.csv"**.</span></span>
    

    
5. <span data-ttu-id="81889-256">单击 "**搜索**" 以使用搜索条件运行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-256">Click **Search** to run the search using your search criteria.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-257">搜索结果将被加载, 并在几分钟后显示在 "**结果**" 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-257">The search results are loaded, and after a few moments they are displayed under **Results**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-258">搜索完成后, 将显示找到的结果数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-258">When the search is finished, the number of results found is displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-259">请注意, 在**结果**窗格中最多可显示5000个事件, 并增加150个事件;如果超过5000个事件满足搜索条件, 则显示最新的5000事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-259">Note that a maximum of 5,000 events will be displayed in the **Results** pane in increments of 150 events; if more than 5,000 events meet the search criteria, the most recent 5,000 events are displayed.</span></span> 
    
    ![搜索完成后显示的结果数](media/986216f1-ca2f-4747-9480-e232b5bf094c.png)
  
  
#### <a name="tips-for-searching-the-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-261">有关搜索审核日志的提示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-261">Tips for searching the audit log</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-262">您可以通过单击活动名称来选择要搜索的特定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-262">You can select specific activities to search for by clicking on the activity name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-263">或者, 您可以通过单击组名称来搜索组中的所有活动 (如**文件和文件夹活动**)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-263">Or you can search for all activities in a group (such as **File and folder activities**) by clicking on the group name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-264">如果已选择活动, 则可以单击它以取消选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-264">If an activity is selected, you can click it to cancel the selection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-265">您还可以使用搜索框显示包含您键入的关键字的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-265">You can also use the search box to display the activities that contain the keyword that you type.</span></span>
    
    ![单击 "活动组名称" 以选择所有活动](media/3cde97cb-6f35-47c0-8612-ecd9c6ac36a3.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-267">您必须在 "**活动**" 列表中选择 "**显示所有活动的结果**" 以显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-267">You have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list to display events from the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-268">此审核日志中的事件在结果的 "**活动**" 列中显示 cmdlet 名称 (例如, "**集-邮箱**")。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-268">Events from this audit log display a cmdlet name (for example, **Set-Mailbox** ) in the **Activity** column in the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-269">有关详细信息, 请单击本主题中的 "已**审核的活动**" 选项卡, 然后单击 " **Exchange 管理活动**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-269">For more information, click the **Audited activities** tab in this topic and then click **Exchange admin activities**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-270">同样, 有些审核活动在 "**活动**" 列表中没有对应的项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-270">Similarly, there are some auditing activities that don't have a corresponding item in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-271">如果您知道这些活动的操作的名称, 则可以搜索所有活动, 然后通过在 "**活动**" 列的框中键入操作的名称来筛选结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-271">If you know the name of the operation for these activities, you can search for all activities, then filter the results by typing the name of the operation in the box for the **Activity** column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-272">有关筛选结果的详细信息, 请参阅[第3步: 筛选搜索结果](#step-3-filter-the-search-results)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-272">See [Step 3: Filter the search results](#step-3-filter-the-search-results) for more information about filtering the results.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-273">单击 "**清除**" 以清除当前搜索条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-273">Click **Clear** to clear the current search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-274">日期范围将恢复为最近七天的默认值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-274">The date range returns to the default of the last seven days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-275">您还可以单击 "全部**清除" 以显示所有活动的结果**, 以取消所有选定活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-275">You can also click **Clear all to show results for all activities** to cancel all selected activities.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-276">如果找到了5000结果, 可能假设有超过5000个事件满足搜索条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-276">If 5,000 results are found, you can probably assume there are more than 5,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-277">您可以优化搜索条件, 然后重新运行搜索以返回较少的结果, 也可以通过选择 "**导出结果** \> " "**下载所有结果**" 来导出所有搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-277">You can either refine the search criteria and rerun the search to return fewer results, or you can export all of the search results by selecting **Export results** \> **Download all results**.</span></span>

  
### <a name="step-2-view-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-278">步骤 2: 查看搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-278">Step 2: View the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-279">审核日志搜索的结果将显示在 "**审核日志搜索**" 页上的 "**结果**" 下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-279">The results of an audit log search are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-280">如前所述, 最大值为 5000 (最新) 事件以150个事件为增量显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-280">As previously stated a maximum of 5,000 (newest) events are displayed in increments of 150 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-281">若要显示更多事件, 可以使用 "**结果**" 窗格中的滚动条, 也可以按**Shift + End**显示接下来的150事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-281">To display more events you can use the scroll bar in the **Results** pane or you can press **Shift + End** to display the next 150 events.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-282">结果中包含有关搜索返回的每个事件的以下信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-282">The results contain the following information about each event returned by the search.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-283">**日期:** 事件发生时的日期和时间 (采用 UTC 格式)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-283">**Date:** The date and time (in UTC format) when the event occurred.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-284">**IP 地址:** 记录活动时使用的设备的 IP 地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-284">**IP address:** The IP address of the device that was used when the activity was logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-285">IP 地址显示为 IPv4 或 IPv6 地址格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-285">The IP address is displayed in either an IPv4 or IPv6 address format.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-286">**用户:** 执行触发事件的操作的用户 (或服务帐户)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-286">**User:** The user (or service account) who performed the action that triggered the event.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-287">**活动:** 用户执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-287">**Activity:** The activity performed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-288">此值与您在 "**活动**" 下拉列表中选择的活动相对应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-288">This value corresponds to the activities that you selected in the **Activities** drop down list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-289">对于来自 Exchange 管理员审核日志的事件, 此列中的值为 Exchange cmdlet。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-289">For an event from the Exchange admin audit log, the value in this column is an Exchange cmdlet.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-290">**项:** 作为对应活动的结果创建或修改的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-290">**Item:** The object that was created or modified as a result of the corresponding activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-291">例如, 已查看或修改的文件或已更新的用户帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-291">For example, the file that was viewed or modified or the user account that was updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-292">此列中并非所有活动都具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-292">Not all activities have a value in this column.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-293">**详细信息:** 有关活动的其他详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-293">**Detail:** Additional detail about an activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-294">同样, 并非所有活动都具有值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-294">Again, not all activities will have a value.</span></span> 
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="81889-295">单击 "**结果**" 下的列标题以对结果进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-295">Click a column header under **Results** to sort the results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-296">您可以按从 A 到 Z 或从 Z 到 A 对结果进行排序。单击**日期**标头可将结果从 "最旧" 或 "降序" 更新为 "最旧"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-296">You can sort the results from A to Z or Z to A. Click the **Date** header to sort the results from oldest to newest or newest to oldest.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="view-the-details-for-a-specific-event"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-297">查看特定事件的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-297">View the details for a specific event</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-298">您可以通过单击搜索结果列表中的事件记录来查看有关事件的更多详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-298">You can view more details about an event by clicking the event record in the list of search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-299">将显示 "**详细信息**" 页, 其中包含事件记录中的详细属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-299">A **Details** page is displayed that contains the detailed properties from the event record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-300">显示的属性取决于事件发生时所采用的 Office 365 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-300">The properties that are displayed depend on the Office 365 service in which the event occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-301">若要显示这些详细信息, 请单击 "**详细信息**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-301">To display these details, click **More information**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-302">有关说明, 请参阅[Office 365 审核日志中的详细属性](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-302">For descriptions, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>
  
![单击 "详细信息" 查看审核日志事件记录的详细属性](media/6df582ae-d339-4735-b1a6-80914fb77a08.png)

  
### <a name="step-3-filter-the-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-304">步骤 3: 筛选搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-304">Step 3: Filter the search results</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-305">除了排序之外, 您还可以筛选审核日志搜索的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-305">In addition to sorting, you can also filter the results of an audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-306">这是一个很好的功能, 可帮助您快速筛选特定用户或活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-306">This is a great feature that can help you quickly filter the results for a specific user or activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-307">您可以先创建宽搜索, 然后快速筛选结果以查看特定事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-307">You can initially create a wide search and then quickly filter the results to see specific events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-308">然后, 您可以缩小搜索条件, 并重新运行搜索以返回更简单、更简明的结果集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-308">Then you can narrow the search criteria and re-run the search to return a smaller, more concise set of results.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-309">筛选结果:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-309">To filter the results:</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="81889-310">运行审核日志搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-310">Run an audit log search.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="81889-311">显示结果后, 单击 "**筛选结果**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-311">When the results are displayed, click **Filter results**.</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-312">关键字框显示在每个列标题下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-312">Keyword boxes are displayed under each column header.</span></span>
    
3. <span data-ttu-id="81889-313">单击列标题下的一个框, 并根据要筛选的列键入一个词或短语。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-313">Click one of the boxes under a column header and type a word or phrase, depending on the column you're filtering on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-314">结果将会动态调整, 以显示与您的筛选器匹配的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-314">The results will dynamically readjust to display the events that match your filter.</span></span>
    
    ![在 filter 中键入 word 以显示与筛选器匹配的事件](media/542dc323-a997-402c-934b-cc5e218e50bc.png)
  
4. <span data-ttu-id="81889-316">若要清除筛选器, 请单击 "筛选器" 框中的 " **X** " 或只单击 "**隐藏筛选**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-316">To clear a filter, click the **X** in the filter box or just click **Hide filtering**.</span></span>
    
> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="81889-317">若要显示 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件, 请**-** 在 "**活动**筛选器" 框中键入 a (短线)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-317">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-318">这将显示在 Exchange 管理员事件的 "**活动**" 列中显示的 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-318">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-319">然后, 您可以按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-319">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 

### <a name="step-4-export-the-search-results-to-a-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-320">步骤 4: 将搜索结果导出到文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-320">Step 4: Export the search results to a file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-321">您可以将审核日志搜索的结果导出到本地计算机上的逗号分隔值 (CSV) 文件中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-321">You can export the results of an audit log search to a comma separated value (CSV) file on your local computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-322">可以在 Microsoft Excel 中打开此文件, 并使用诸如搜索、排序、筛选和拆分单个列 (包含多个属性) 的多个列中的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-322">You can open this file in Microsoft Excel and use features such as search, sorting, filtering, and splitting a single column (that contains multiple properties) into multiple columns.</span></span>
  
1. <span data-ttu-id="81889-323">运行审核日志搜索, 然后修改搜索条件, 直到获得所需的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-323">Run an audit log search, and then revise the search criteria until you have the desired results.</span></span>
    
2. <span data-ttu-id="81889-324">单击 "**导出结果**", 然后选择下列选项之一:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-324">Click **Export results** and select one of the following options:</span></span> 
    
     - <span data-ttu-id="81889-325">**保存加载的结果**–选择此选项可仅导出在 "**审核日志搜索**" 页上的 "**结果**" 下显示的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-325">**Save loaded results** – Choose this option to export only the entries that are displayed under **Results** on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-326">下载的 CSV 文件包含页面上显示的相同列 (和数据) (日期、用户、活动、项和详细信息)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-326">The CSV file that is downloaded contains the same columns (and data) displayed on the page (Date, User, Activity, Item, and Details).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-327">包含来自审核日志条目的详细信息的 CSV 文件中包含其他列 (称为 "**更多**")。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-327">An additional column (named **More**) is included in the CSV file that contains more information from the audit log entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-328">因为您要导出的结果与在**审核日志搜索**页面上加载 (和查看) 的结果相同, 所以最多可以导出5000个条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-328">Because you're exporting the same results that are loaded (and viewable) on the **Audit log search** page, a maximum of 5,000 entries are exported.</span></span> 
    
     - <span data-ttu-id="81889-329">**下载所有结果**–选择此选项可导出符合搜索条件的 Office 365 审核日志中的所有条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-329">**Download all results** – Choose this option to export all entries from the Office 365 audit log that meet the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-330">对于较大的搜索结果集, 请选择此选项从审核日志中下载所有条目, 除了可在 "**审核日志搜索**" 页上显示的5000审核记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-330">For a large set of search results, choose this option to download all entries from the audit log in addition to the 5,000 audit records that can be displayed on the **Audit log search** page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-331">此选项将从审核日志中将原始数据下载到 CSV 文件, 并包含来自名为**AuditData**的列中的审核日志条目的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-331">This option will download the raw data from the audit log to a CSV file, and contains additional information from the audit log entry in a column named **AuditData**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-332">如果选择此导出选项, 可能需要较长时间下载文件, 因为如果选择其他选项, 文件可能会比下载的文件大得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-332">It may take longer to download the file if you choose this export option because the file may be much larger than the one that's downloaded if you choose the other option.</span></span>
    
       > [!IMPORTANT]
       > <span data-ttu-id="81889-333">您可以从单个审核日志搜索中最多将50000个条目下载到 CSV 文件中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-333">You can download a maximum of 50,000 entries to a CSV file from a single audit log search.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-334">如果将50000条目下载到 CSV 文件中, 您可能会假定有超过50000个事件满足搜索条件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-334">If 50,000 entries are downloaded to the CSV file, you can probably assume there are more than 50,000 events that met the search criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-335">若要导出超过此限制, 请尝试使用日期范围来减少审核日志条目的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-335">To export more than this limit, try using a date range to reduce the number of audit log entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-336">您可能需要运行包含较小日期范围的多个搜索以导出50000个以上的条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-336">You might have to run multiple searches with smaller date ranges to export more than 50,000 entries.</span></span> 
  
3. <span data-ttu-id="81889-337">选择 "导出" 选项后, 将在窗口底部显示一条消息, 提示您打开 CSV 文件, 将其保存到 "下载" 文件夹中, 或将其保存到特定文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-337">After you select an export option, a message is displayed at the bottom of the window that prompts you to open the CSV file, save it to the Downloads folder, or save it to a specific folder.</span></span>
 
#### <a name="more-information-about-exporting-and-viewing-audit-log-search-results"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-338">有关导出和查看审核日志搜索结果的详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-338">More information about exporting and viewing audit log search results</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-339">如果下载所有搜索结果, 则 CSV 文件中包含一个名为 " **AuditData**" 的列, 其中包含有关每个事件的其他信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-339">If you download all search results, the CSV file contains a column named **AuditData**, which contains additional information about each event.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-340">此列中的数据由一个 JSON 对象组成, 该对象包含审核日志记录中的多个属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-340">The data in this column consists of a JSON object that contains multiple properties from the audit log record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-341">JSON 对象中的每个*属性: 值*对都以逗号分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-341">Each *property:value* pair in the JSON object are separated by a comma.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-342">您可以使用 Excel 中 Power Query 编辑器中的 JSON 转换工具将**AuditData**列拆分为多个列, 以便 JSON 对象中的每个属性都有自己的列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-342">You can use the JSON transform tool in the Power Query Editor in Excel to split **AuditData** column into multiple columns so that each property in the JSON object has its own column.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-343">这将允许您对其中一个或多个属性进行排序和筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-343">This will let you sort and filter on one or more of these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-344">有关使用 Power Query 编辑器转换 JSON 对象的分步说明, 请参阅[导出、配置和查看审核日志记录](export-view-audit-log-records.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-344">For step-by-step instructions using the Power Query Editor to transform the JSON object, see [Export, configure, and view audit log records](export-view-audit-log-records.md).</span></span>
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-345">拆分**AuditData**列后, 可以在 "**操作**" 列上进行筛选, 以显示特定类型的活动的详细属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-345">After you split the **AuditData** column, you can filter on the **Operations** column to display the detailed properties for a specific type of activity.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-346">"**下载所有结果**" 选项将原始数据从 Office 365 审核日志下载到 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-346">The **Download all results** option downloads the raw data from the Office 365 audit log to a CSV file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-347">如果您选择 "**保存加载的结果**" 选项, 则此文件包含的列名称 (CreationDate、UserIds、Operation、AuditData) 不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-347">This file contains different column names (CreationDate, UserIds, Operation, AuditData) than the file that's downloaded if you select the **Save loaded results** option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-348">同一活动的两个不同的 CSV 文件中的值也可能不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-348">The values in the two different CSV files for the same activity may also be different.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-349">例如, CSV 文件的 "**操作**" 列中的活动和 "用户友好" 名称的值可能与**审核日志搜索**页上的 "**活动**" 列中显示的名称不同;例如, Mailboxlogin 该值与登录到邮箱的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-349">For example, the activity in the **Action** column in the CSV file and may have a different value than the "user-friendly" name that's displayed in the **Activity** column on the **Audit log search** page; for example, MailboxLogin vs. User signed in to mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-350">从包含来自不同 Office 365 服务的事件的搜索查询中下载所有结果时, CSV 文件中的 " **AuditData** " 列包含不同的属性, 具体取决于执行操作所使用的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-350">When you download all results from a search query that contains events from different Office 365 services, the **AuditData** column in the CSV file contains different properties depending on which service the action was performed in.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-351">例如, Exchange 和 Azure AD 审核日志中的条目包含一个名为**ResultStatus**的属性, 用于指示操作是否成功。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-351">For example, entries from Exchange and Azure AD audit logs include a property named **ResultStatus** that indicates if the action was successful or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-352">此属性不包含在 SharePoint 中的事件中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-352">This property isn't included for events in SharePoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-353">同样, SharePoint 事件具有一个属性, 用于标识与文件和文件夹相关的活动的网站 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-353">Similarly, SharePoint events have a property that identifies the site URL for file and folder related activities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-354">若要缓解此行为, 请考虑使用不同的搜索从单个服务中导出活动的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-354">To mitigate this behavior, consider using different searches to export the results for activities from a single service.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="81889-355">有关在下载所有结果和每个结果适用的服务时, 在 CSV 文件的**AuditData**列中列出的许多属性的说明, 请参阅[Office 365 审核日志中的详细属性](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-355">For a description of many of the properties that are listed in the **AuditData** column in the CSV file when you download all results, and the service each one applies to, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>

## <a name="audited-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-356">审核的活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-356">Audited activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-357">本节中的表介绍了在 Office 365 中审核的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-357">The tables in this section describe the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-358">您可以通过在安全与合规中心中搜索审核日志来搜索这些事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-358">You can search for these events by searching the audit log in the security and compliance center.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-359">这些表对相关活动或特定 Office 365 服务中的活动进行分组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-359">These tables group related activities or the activities from a specific Office 365 service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-360">这些表包括在 "**活动**" 下拉列表中显示的友好名称, 以及在导出搜索结果时, 在审核记录的详细信息和 CSV 文件中显示的相应操作的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-360">The tables include the friendly name that's displayed in the **Activities** drop-down list and the name of the corresponding operation that appears in the detailed information of an audit record and in the CSV file when you export the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-361">有关详细信息的说明, 请参阅[Office 365 审核日志中的详细属性](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-361">For descriptions of the detailed information, see [Detailed properties in the Office 365 audit log](detailed-properties-in-the-office-365-audit-log.md).</span></span>
