### <a name="file-and-page-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-387">文件和页面活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-387">File and page activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-388">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件和页面活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-388">The following table describes the file and page activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-389">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-389">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-390">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-390">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-391">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-391">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-392">访问的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-392">Accessed file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-393">FileAccessed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-393">FileAccessed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-394">用户或系统帐户访问文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-394">User or system account accesses a file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-395">（无）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-395">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-396">FileAccessedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-396">FileAccessedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-397">这与 "访问的文件" (FileAccessed) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-397">This is related to the "Accessed file" (FileAccessed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-398">当同一人持续访问一个文件长时间 (最长为3小时) 时, 将记录 FileAccessedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-398">A FileAccessedExtended event is logged when the same person continually accesses a file for an extended period of time (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-399">记录 FileAccessedExtended 事件的目的是减少在连续访问文件时记录的 FileAccessed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-399">The purpose of logging FileAccessedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileAccessed events that are logged when a file is continually accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-400">这有助于减少多个 FileAccessed 记录在本质上是相同的用户活动的噪音, 并让您重点关注最初的 (更重要的) FileAccessed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-400">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileAccessed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileAccessed event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-401">更改了合规性策略标签</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-401">Changed compliance policy label</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-402">ComplianceSettingChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-402">ComplianceSettingChanged</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-403">保留标签应用于文档或从文档中删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-403">A retention label was applied to or removed from a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-404">手动或自动将保留标签应用于邮件时, 将触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-404">This event is triggered when a retention label is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-405">将记录状态更改为 "已锁定"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-405">Changed record status to locked</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-406">LockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-406">LockRecord</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-407">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态被锁定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-407">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was locked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-408">这意味着无法修改或删除该文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-408">This means the document can't be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-409">只有为网站至少分配了 "参与者" 权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-409">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-410">将记录状态更改为 "已解锁"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-410">Changed record status to unlocked</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-411">UnlockRecord</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-411">UnlockRecord</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-412">将文档分类为记录的保留标签的记录状态被解除锁定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-412">The record status of a retention label that classifies a document as a record was unlocked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-413">这意味着可以修改或删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-413">This means the document can be modified or deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-414">只有为网站至少分配了 "参与者" 权限的用户才能更改文档的记录状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-414">Only users assigned at least the contributor permission for a site can change the record status of a document.</span></span><br/><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-415">签入文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-415">Checked in file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-416">FileCheckedIn</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-416">FileCheckedIn</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-417">用户签入文档库中签出的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-417">User checks in a document that they checked out from a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-418">签出文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-418">Checked out file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-419">FileCheckedOut</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-419">FileCheckedOut</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-420">用户签出位于文档库中的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-420">User checks out a document located in a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-421">用户可以对与其共享的文档执行签出和更改操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-421">Users can check out and make changes to documents that have been shared with them.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-422">复制的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-422">Copied file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-423">FileCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-423">FileCopied</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-424">用户从网站复制文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-424">User copies a document from a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-425">可以将复制的文件保存到网站上的另一个文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-425">The copied file can be saved to another folder on the site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-426">删除的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-426">Deleted file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-427">FileDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-427">FileDeleted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-428">用户从网站中删除文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-428">User deletes a document from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-429">从回收站删除的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-429">Deleted file from recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-430">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-430">FileDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-431">用户从网站的回收站中删除文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-431">User deletes a file from the recycle bin of a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-432">从第二阶段回收站删除的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-432">Deleted file from second-stage recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-433">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-433">FileDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-434">用户从网站的第二阶段回收站中删除文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-434">User deletes a file from the second-stage recycle bin of a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-435">已删除记录合规性策略标签</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-435">Deleted record compliance policy label</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-436">ComplianceRecordDelete</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-436">ComplianceRecordDelete</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-437">已删除作为记录分类的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-437">A document that was classified as a record was deleted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-438">在将内容分类为记录的保留标签应用于文档时, 该文档被视为一条记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-438">A document is considered a record when a retention label that classifies content as a record is applied to the document.</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-439">检测到的文档敏感度不匹配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-439">Detected document sensitivity mismatch</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-440">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-440">DocumentSensitivityMismatchDetected</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-441">用户上载使用敏感度标签分级的文档, 该文档的优先级高于将文档上载到的网站所应用的敏感度标签。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-441">User uploads a document classified with a sensitivity label that has a higher priority than the sensitivity label that's applied to the site the document is uploaded to.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-442">注释如果应用于网站的敏感度标签的优先级高于应用于上载到网站的文档的敏感度标签, 则不会触发此事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-442">Note this event isn't triggered if the sensitivity label applied to a site has a higher priority than the sensitivity label applied to a document that's uploaded to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-443">有关敏感度标签优先级的详细信息, 请参阅[敏感度标签概述](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters)中的 "标签优先级" 一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-443">For more information about sensitivity label priority, see the "Label priority" section in [Overview of sensitivity labels](sensitivity-labels.md#label-priority-order-matters).</span></span><br/>|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-444">在文件中检测到恶意软件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-444">Detected malware in file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-445">FileMalwareDetected</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-445">FileMalwareDetected</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-446">SharePoint 防病毒引擎可检测文件中的恶意软件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-446">SharePoint anti-virus engine detects malware in a file.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-447">放弃文件签出</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-447">Discarded file checkout</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-448">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-448">FileCheckOutDiscarded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-p157">用户放弃（或撤消）签出的文件。这意味着将放弃签出文件时对其所做的更改，而不将其保存到文档库中的文档版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-p157">User discards (or undos) a checked out file. That means any changes they made to the file when it was checked out are discarded, and not saved to the version of the document in the document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-451">下载文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-451">Downloaded file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-452">FileDownloaded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-452">FileDownloaded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-453">用户从网站下载文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-453">User downloads a document from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-454">修改的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-454">Modified file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-455">FileModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-455">FileModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-456">用户或系统帐户修改位于网站上的文档的内容或属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-456">User or system account modifies the content or the properties of a document located on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-457">（无）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-457">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-458">FileModifiedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-458">FileModifiedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-459">这与 "修改的文件" (FileModified) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-459">This is related to the "Modified file" (FileModified) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-460">当同一人持续修改一个文件长时间 (最长为3小时) 时, 将记录 FileModifiedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-460">A FileModifiedExtended event is logged when the same person continually modifies a file for an extended period of time (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-461">记录 FileModifiedExtended 事件的目的是减少文件被连续修改时记录的 FileModified 事件的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-461">The purpose of logging FileModifiedExtended events is to reduce the number of FileModified events that are logged when a file is continually modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-462">这有助于减少多个 FileModified 记录在本质上是相同的用户活动的噪音, 并让您重点关注最初的 (更重要的) FileModified 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-462">This helps reduce the noise of multiple FileModified records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) FileModified event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-463">移动的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-463">Moved file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-464">FileMoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-464">FileMoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-465">用户将文档从其在网站上的当前位置移动到新位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-465">User moves a document from its current location on a site to a new location.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-466">已回收文件的所有次要版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-466">Recycled all minor versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-467">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-467">FileVersionsAllMinorsRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-468">用户从文件的版本历史记录中删除所有次要版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-468">User deletes all minor versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-469">已删除的版本将移至网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-469">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-470">文件的所有版本都已回收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-470">Recycled all versions of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-471">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-471">FileVersionsAllRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-472">用户从文件的版本历史记录中删除所有版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-472">User deletes all versions from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-473">已删除的版本将移至网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-473">The deleted versions are moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-474">文件的已回收版本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-474">Recycled version of file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-475">FileVersionRecycled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-475">FileVersionRecycled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-476">用户从文件的版本历史记录中删除版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-476">User deletes a version from the version history of a file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-477">删除的版本将移至网站的回收站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-477">The deleted version is moved to the site's recycle bin.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-478">重命名文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-478">Renamed file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-479">FileRenamed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-479">FileRenamed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-480">用户重命名网站上的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-480">User renames a document on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-481">还原的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-481">Restored file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-482">FileRestored</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-482">FileRestored</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-483">用户从网站的回收站还原文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-483">User restores a document from the recycle bin of a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-484">上载的文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-484">Uploaded file</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-485">FileUploaded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-485">FileUploaded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-486">用户将文档上载到网站上的文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-486">User uploads a document to a folder on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-487">查看页面</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-487">Viewed page</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-488">PageViewed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-488">PageViewed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-489">用户查看网站上的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-489">User views a page on a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-490">这不包括使用 Web 浏览器查看位于文档库中的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-490">This doesn't include using a Web browser to view files located in a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-491">（无）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-491">(none)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-492">PageViewedExtended</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-492">PageViewedExtended</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-493">这与 "查看过的页面" (PageViewed) 活动相关。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-493">This is related to the "Viewed page" (PageViewed) activity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-494">当同一人持续查看某个网页长时间 (最长为3小时) 时, 将记录 PageViewedExtended 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-494">A PageViewedExtended event is logged when the same person continually views a web page for an extended period of time (up to 3 hours).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-495">记录 PageViewedExtended 事件的目的是减少在连续查看页面时记录的 PageViewed 事件数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-495">The purpose of logging PageViewedExtended events is to reduce the number of PageViewed events that are logged when a page is continually viewed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-496">这有助于减少多个 PageViewed 记录在本质上是相同的用户活动的噪音, 并让您重点关注最初的 (更重要的) PageViewed 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-496">This helps reduce the noise of multiple PageViewed records for what is essentially the same user activity, and lets you focus on the initial (and more important) PageViewed event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-497">查看客户端的信号</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-497">View signaled by client</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-498">ClientViewSignaled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-498">ClientViewSignaled</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-499">用户的客户端 (如网站或移动应用程序) 已通知用户已查看指定的页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-499">A user’s client (such as website or mobile app) has signaled that the indicated page has been viewed by the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-500">此活动通常会在页面的 PagePrefetched 事件后记录下来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-500">This activity is often logged following a PagePrefetched event for a page.</span></span> <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="81889-501">**注意**: 由于 ClientViewSignaled 事件由客户端 (而不是服务器) 发出通知, 因此该事件可能不会被服务器记录, 因此可能不会出现在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-501">**NOTE**: Because ClientViewSignaled events are signaled by the client, rather than the server, it's possible the event may not be logged by the server and therefore may not appear in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-502">审核记录中的信息也可能不可信。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-502">It's also possible that information in the audit record may not be trustworthy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-503">但是, 由于用户的标识由用于创建信号的令牌进行验证, 因此相应的审核记录中列出的用户标识是准确的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-503">However, because the user’s identity is validated by the token used to create the signal, the user’s identity listed in the corresponding audit record is accurate.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-504">（无）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-504">(none)</span></span> <br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-505">PagePrefetched</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-505">PagePrefetched</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-506">用户的客户端 (如网站或移动应用程序) 已请求指示的页面, 以便在用户浏览到它时帮助提高性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-506">A user’s client (such as website or mobile app) has requested the indicated page to help improve performance if the user browses to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-507">记录此事件以指示页面内容已提供给用户的客户端;此事件不是用户实际导航到页面的明确指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-507">This event is logged to indicate the page content has been served to the user’s client; this event isn't a definitive indication that the user actually navigated to the page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-508">当客户端呈现页面内容时 (根据用户的请求), 应生成一个 ClientViewSignaled 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-508">When the page content is rendered by the client (as per the user’s request) a ClientViewSignaled event should be generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-509">请注意, 并非所有客户端都支持指示预回迁, 因此某些预回迁的活动可能改为作为 PageViewed 事件进行记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-509">Note that not all clients support indicating a pre-fetch, and therefore some pre-fetched activities might instead be logged as PageViewed events.</span></span><br/>|
||||
  
### <a name="folder-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-510">文件夹活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-510">Folder activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-511">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件夹活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-511">The following table describes the folder activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-512">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-512">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-513">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-513">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-514">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-514">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-515">复制的文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-515">Copied folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-516">FolderCopied</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-516">FolderCopied</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-517">用户将文件夹从网站复制到 SharePoint 或 OneDrive for Business 中的其他位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-517">User copies a folder from a site to another location in SharePoint or OneDrive for Business.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-518">创建的文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-518">Created folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-519">FolderCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-519">FolderCreated</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-520">用户在网站上创建一个文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-520">User creates a folder on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-521">已删除文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-521">Deleted folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-522">FolderDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-522">FolderDeleted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-523">用户从网站中删除文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-523">User deletes a folder from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-524">回收站中已删除的文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-524">Deleted folder from recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-525">FolderDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-525">FolderDeletedFirstStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-526">用户从网站的回收站中删除文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-526">User deletes a folder from the recycle bin on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-527">从第二阶段回收站删除的文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-527">Deleted folder from second-stage recycle bin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-528">FolderDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-528">FolderDeletedSecondStageRecycleBin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-529">用户从网站的第二阶段回收站中删除文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-529">User deletes a folder from the second-stage recycle bin on a site.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="sharing-and-access-request-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-616">共享和访问请求活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-616">Sharing and access request activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-617">下表介绍了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的用户共享和访问请求活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-617">The following table describes the user sharing and access request activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-618">对于共享事件, "**结果**" 下的 "**详细信息**" 列标识与该项目共享的用户或组的名称, 以及该用户或组是否为组织中的成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-618">For sharing events, the **Detail** column under **Results** identifies the name of the user or group the item was shared with and whether that user or group is a member or guest in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-619">有关详细信息, 请参阅[在 Office 365 审核日志中使用共享审核](use-sharing-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-619">For more information, see [Use sharing auditing in the Office 365 audit log](use-sharing-auditing.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="81889-620">根据 user 对象的 UserType 属性, 用户可以是*成员*或*来宾*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-620">Users can be either  *members*  or  *guests*  based on the UserType property of the user object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-621">成员通常是员工, 而来宾通常是组织外部的合作者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-621">A member is usually an employee, and a guest is usually a collaborator outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-622">当用户接受共享邀请 (而不是组织的一部分) 时, 将在组织的目录中为其创建来宾帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-622">When a user accepts a sharing invitation (and isn't already part of your organization), a guest account is created for them in your organization's directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-623">一旦来宾用户在目录中拥有帐户, 资源就可以直接与他们共享 (无需邀请)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-623">Once the guest user has an account in your directory, resources may be shared directly with them (without requiring an invitation).</span></span> 
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-624">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-624">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-625">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-625">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-626">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-626">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-627">向网站集添加了权限级别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-627">Added permission level to site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-628">PermissionLevelAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-628">PermissionLevelAdded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-629">向网站集添加了权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-629">A permission level was added to a site collection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-630">接受的访问请求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-630">Accepted access request</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-631">AccessRequestAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-631">AccessRequestAccepted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-632">接受对网站、文件夹或文档的访问请求, 并向请求用户授予访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-632">An access request to a site, folder, or document was accepted and the requesting user has been granted access.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-633">接受的共享邀请</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-633">Accepted sharing invitation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-634">SharingInvitationAccepted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-634">SharingInvitationAccepted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-635">用户 (成员或来宾) 接受了共享邀请, 并且已被授予对资源的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-635">User (member or guest) accepted a sharing invitation and was granted access to a resource.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-636">此事件包括受邀的用户的相关信息, 以及用于接受邀请的电子邮件地址 (可以是不同的)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-636">This event includes information about the user who was invited and the email address that was used to accept the invitation (they could be different).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-637">此活动通常附带第二个事件, 该事件描述了如何向用户授予对资源的访问权限, 例如, 将用户添加到有权访问该资源的组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-637">This activity is often accompanied by a second event that describes how the user was granted access to the resource, for example, adding the user to a group that has access to the resource.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-638">阻止的共享邀请</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-638">Blocked sharing invitation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-639">SharingInvitationBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-639">SharingInvitationBlocked</span></span>  <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="81889-640">由于外部共享策略允许或拒绝基于目标用户的域的外部共享, 因此组织中的用户发送的共享邀请被阻止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-640">A sharing invitation sent by a user in your organization is blocked because of an external sharing policy that either allows or denies external sharing based on the domain of the target user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-641">在这种情况下, 共享邀请被阻止, 因为:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-641">In this case, the sharing invitation was blocked because:</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-642">目标用户的域不包含在允许的域的列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-642">The target user's domain isn't included in the list of allowed domains.</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-643">或</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-643">Or</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-644">目标用户的域包含在阻止域的列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-644">The target user's domain is included in the list of blocked domains.</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-645">有关允许或阻止基于域的外部共享的详细信息, 请参阅[SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive For business 中的受限制域共享](https://support.office.com/article/5d7589cd-0997-4a00-a2ba-2320ec49c4e9)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-645">For more information about allowing or blocking external sharing based on domains, see [Restricted domains sharing in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business](https://support.office.com/article/5d7589cd-0997-4a00-a2ba-2320ec49c4e9).</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="synchronization-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-715">同步活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-715">Synchronization activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-716">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive for Business 中的文件同步活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-716">The following table lists file synchronization activities in SharePoint Online and OneDrive for Business.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-717">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-717">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-718">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-718">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-719">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-719">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-720">允许的计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-720">Allowed computer to sync files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-721">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-721">ManagedSyncClientAllowed</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-722">用户与网站成功建立同步关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-722">User successfully establishes a sync relationship with a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-723">同步关系成功, 因为用户的计算机是已添加到可以访问组织中的文档库的域列表 (称为 "*安全收件人列表*") 的域的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-723">The sync relationship is successful because the user's computer is a member of a domain that's been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list*  ) that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="81889-724">有关此功能的详细信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-724">For more information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-725">阻止的计算机同步文件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-725">Blocked computer from syncing files</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-726">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-726">UnmanagedSyncClientBlocked</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-727">用户尝试与不是组织域成员的计算机或域的成员建立同步关系, 而该计算机尚未添加到可以访问文档的域列表 (称为*安全收件人列表)* 。组织中的库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-727">User tries to establish a sync relationship with a site from a computer that isn't a member of your organization's domain or is a member of a domain that hasn't been added to the list of domains (called the  *safe recipients list)*  that can access document libraries in your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-728">不允许同步关系，并阻止用户计算机在文档库上同步、下载或上传文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-728">The sync relationship is not allowed, and the user's computer is blocked from syncing, downloading, or uploading files on a document library.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="81889-729">有关此功能的信息，请参阅[使用 Windows PowerShell cmdlet 为安全收件人列表中的域启用 OneDrive 同步](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-729">For information about this feature, see [Use Windows PowerShell cmdlets to enable OneDrive sync for domains that are on the safe recipients list](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=534609).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-730">将文件下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-730">Downloaded files to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-731">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-731">FileSyncDownloadedFull</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-732">用户建立同步关系, 并首次成功从文档库中将文件下载到其计算机。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-732">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully downloads files for the first time to their computer from a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-733">已将文件更改下载到计算机</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-733">Downloaded file changes to computer</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-734">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-734">FileSyncDownloadedPartial</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-735">用户成功地从文档库中下载对文件所做的任何更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-735">User successfully downloads any changes to files from a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-736">此活动指示对文档库中的文件所做的任何更改都将下载到用户的计算机上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-736">This activity indicates that any changes that were made to files in the document library were downloaded to the user's computer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-737">仅下载了所做的更改, 因为文档库先前已由用户下载 (由**下载的文件到计算机**活动中所示)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-737">Only changes were downloaded because the document library was previously downloaded by the user (as indicated by the **Downloaded files to computer** activity).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-738">将文件上载到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-738">Uploaded files to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-739">FileSyncUploadedFull</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-739">FileSyncUploadedFull</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-740">用户建立同步关系, 并将第一次成功地将文件从计算机上载到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-740">User establishes a sync relationship and successfully uploads files for the first time from their computer to a document library.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-741">将文件更改上载到文档库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-741">Uploaded file changes to document library</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-742">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-742">FileSyncUploadedPartial</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-743">用户成功地将更改上载到文档库上的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-743">User successfully uploads changes to files on a document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-744">此事件表明对文档库文件的本地版本所做的任何更改都已成功上传到文档库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-744">This event indicates that any changes made to the local version of a file from a document library are successfully uploaded to the document library.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-745">仅上载更改, 因为用户之前已上载这些文件 (由 "**上载的文件到文档库**" 活动中所示)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-745">Only changes are uploaded because those files were previously uploaded by the user (as indicated by the **Uploaded files to document library** activity).</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="site-permissions-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-746">网站权限活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-746">Site permissions activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-747">下表列出了与在 SharePoint 中分配权限以及使用组授予 (和废除) 对网站的访问权限的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-747">The following table lists events related to assigning permissions in SharePoint and using groups to give (and revoke) access to sites.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-748">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-748">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-749">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-749">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-750">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-750">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-751">添加了网站集管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-751">Added site collection admin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-752">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-752">SiteCollectionAdminAdded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-753">网站集管理员或所有者向网站的网站集管理员添加人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-753">Site collection administrator or owner adds a person as a site collection administrator for a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-754">网站集管理员具有网站集和所有子网站的完全控制权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-754">Site collection administrators have full control permissions for the site collection and all subsites.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-755">当管理员为自己提供了对用户的 OneDrive 帐户的访问权限 (通过在 SharePoint 管理中心中编辑用户配置文件或[使用 Microsoft 365 管理中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data#part-1---get-access-to-the-former-employees-onedrive-for-business-documents)) 时, 也会记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-755">This activity is also logged when an admin gives themselves access to a user's OneDrive account (by editing the user profile in the SharePoint admin center or  [by using the Microsoft 365 admin center](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/admin/add-users/get-access-to-and-back-up-a-former-user-s-data#part-1---get-access-to-the-former-employees-onedrive-for-business-documents)).</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-756">向 SharePoint 组添加用户或组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-756">Added user or group to SharePoint group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-757">AddedToGroup</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-757">AddedToGroup</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-758">用户向 SharePoint 组添加了成员或来宾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-758">User added a member or guest to a SharePoint group.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-759">这可能是一个有意的操作, 也可能是另一个活动 (如共享事件) 的结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-759">This might have been an intentional action or the result of another activity, such as a sharing event.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-760">中断权限级别继承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-760">Broke permission level inheritance</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-761">PermissionLevelsInheritanceBroken</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-761">PermissionLevelsInheritanceBroken</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-762">更改了某个项目, 因此它不再继承其父项的权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-762">An item was changed so that it no longer inherits permission levels from its parent.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-763">中断共享继承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-763">Broke sharing inheritance</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-764">SharingInheritanceBroken</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-764">SharingInheritanceBroken</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-765">更改了某个项目, 因此它不再继承其父项的共享权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-765">An item was changed so that it no longer inherits sharing permissions from its parent.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-771">删除的组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-771">Deleted group</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-772">GroupRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-772">GroupRemoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-773">用户从网站中删除组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-773">User deletes a group from a site.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-780">网站集上的修改的权限级别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-780">Modified permission level on site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-781">PermissionLevelModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-781">PermissionLevelModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-782">在网站集上更改了权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-782">A permission level was changed on a site collection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-783">修改的网站权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-783">Modified site permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-784">SitePermissionsModified</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-784">SitePermissionsModified</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-785">网站管理员或所有者 (或系统帐户) 更改分配给网站上的组的权限级别。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-785">Site administrator or owner (or system account) changes the permission level that are assigned to a group on a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-786">如果从组中删除了所有权限, 也会记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-786">This activity is also logged if all permissions are removed from a group.</span></span>  <br/><br/> <span data-ttu-id="81889-787">**注意**: 此操作已在 SharePoint Online 中弃用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-787">**NOTE**: This operation has been deprecated in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-788">若要查找相关事件, 可以搜索其他与权限相关的活动, 如**添加的网站集管理员**、向**SharePoint 组添加用户或组**、**允许用户创建组**、**创建组**和**删除组。**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-788">To find related events, you can search for other permission-related activities such as **Added site collection admin**, **Added user or group to SharePoint group**, **Allowed user to create groups**, **Created group**, and **Deleted group.**</span></span>|

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-792">已删除网站集管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-792">Removed site collection admin</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-793">SiteCollectionAdminRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-793">SiteCollectionAdminRemoved</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-794">网站集管理员或所有者将用户作为网站的网站集管理员删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-794">Site collection administrator or owner removes a person as a site collection administrator for a site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-795">当管理员从用户的 OneDrive 帐户的网站集管理员列表中删除自己 (通过在 SharePoint 管理中心中编辑用户配置文件) 时, 也会记录此活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-795">This activity is also logged when an admin removes themselves from the list of site collection administrators for a user's OneDrive account (by editing the user profile in the SharePoint admin center).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-796">请注意, 若要在审核日志搜索结果中返回此活动, 您必须搜索所有活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-796">Note that to return this activity in the audit log search results, you have to search for all activities.</span></span> <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-801">请求的网站管理员权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-801">Requested site admin permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-802">SiteAdminChangeRequest</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-802">SiteAdminChangeRequest</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-803">要添加为网站集的网站集管理员的用户请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-803">User requests to be added as a site collection administrator for a site collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-804">网站集管理员具有网站集和所有子网站的完全控制权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-804">Site collection administrators have full control permissions for the site collection and all subsites.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="site-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-812">网站管理活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-812">Site administration activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-813">下表列出了 SharePoint Online 中的网站管理任务所产生的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-813">The following table lists events that result from site administration tasks in SharePoint Online.</span></span>
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-814">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-814">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-815">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-815">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-816">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-816">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-817">添加了允许的数据位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-817">Added allowed data location</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-818">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-818">AllowedDataLocationAdded</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-819">SharePoint 或全局管理员在多地理位置环境中添加了允许的数据位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-819">A SharePoint or global administrator added an allowed data location in a multi-geo environment.</span></span> <br/>|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-820">添加了豁免用户代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-820">Added exempt user agent</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-821">ExemptUserAgentSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-821">ExemptUserAgentSet</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-822">SharePoint 或全局管理员向 SharePoint 管理中心内的豁免用户代理列表中添加了一个用户代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-822">A SharePoint or global administrator added a user agent to the list of exempt user agents in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-823">添加了地理位置管理员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-823">Added geo location admin</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-824">GeoAdminAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-824">GeoAdminAdded</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-825">SharePoint 或全局管理员将用户添加为位置的地理位置管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-825">A SharePoint or global administrator added a user as a geo admin of a location.</span></span> <br/>|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-826">允许用户创建组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-826">Allowed user to create groups</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-827">AllowGroupCreationSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-827">AllowGroupCreationSet</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-828">网站管理员或所有者向网站添加权限级别, 允许分配该权限的用户为该网站创建组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-828">Site administrator or owner adds a permission level to a site that allows a user assigned that permission to create a group for that site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-829">取消的网站地理位置移动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-829">Cancelled site geo move</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-830">SiteGeoMoveCancelled</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-830">SiteGeoMoveCancelled</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-831">SharePoint 或全局管理员成功取消 SharePoint 或 OneDrive 站点地理位置移动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-831">A SharePoint or global administrator successfully cancels a SharePoint or OneDrive site geo move.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-832">多地理位置功能可让 Office 365 组织跨多个 Office 365 数据中心地理位置, 这些地理位置称为信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-832">The Multi-Geo capability lets an Office 365 organization span multiple Office 365 datacenter geographies, which are called geos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-833">有关详细信息, 请参阅[Office 365 中的 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 中的多地理位置功能](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-833">For more information, see [Multi-Geo Capabilities in OneDrive and SharePoint Online in Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-834">更改了共享策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-834">Changed a sharing policy</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-835">SharingPolicyChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-835">SharingPolicyChanged</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-836">SharePoint 或全局管理员使用 Office 365 管理门户、SharePoint 管理门户或 SharePoint Online 命令行管理程序更改了 SharePoint 共享策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-836">A SharePoint or global administrator changed a SharePoint sharing policy by using the Office 365 admin portal, SharePoint admin portal, or SharePoint Online Management Shell.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-837">将记录对组织中共享策略中的设置所做的任何更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-837">Any change to the settings in the sharing policy in your organization will be logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-838">已更改的策略在事件记录的详细属性中的 " **ModifiedProperties** " 字段中进行标识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-838">The policy that was changed is identified in the **ModifiedProperties** field in the detailed properties of the event record.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-839">已更改设备访问策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-839">Changed device access policy</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-840">DeviceAccessPolicyChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-840">DeviceAccessPolicyChanged</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-841">SharePoint 或全局管理员更改了贵组织的非托管设备策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-841">A SharePoint or global administrator changed the unmanaged devices policy for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-842">此策略可控制不加入您的组织的设备对 SharePoint、OneDrive 和 Office 365 的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-842">This policy controls access to SharePoint, OneDrive, and Office 365 from devices that aren't joined to your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-843">配置此策略需要企业移动性 + 安全性订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-843">Configuring this policy requires an Enterprise Mobility + Security subscription.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-844">有关详细信息，请参阅[控制非托管设备的访问](https://support.office.com/article/5ae550c4-bd20-4257-847b-5c20fb053622)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-844">For more information, see [Control access from unmanaged devices](https://support.office.com/article/5ae550c4-bd20-4257-847b-5c20fb053622).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-845">已更改的豁免用户代理</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-845">Changed exempt user agents</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-846">CustomizeExemptUsers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-846">CustomizeExemptUsers</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-847">SharePoint 或全局管理员自定义了 SharePoint 管理中心内的豁免用户代理列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-847">A SharePoint or global administrator customized the list of exempt user agents in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-848">您可以指定哪些用户代理免于接收整个网页进行索引编制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-848">You can specify which user agents to exempt from receiving an entire web page to index.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-849">这意味着当您指定为豁免的用户代理遇到 InfoPath 表单时, 该表单将作为 XML 文件而不是整个网页返回。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-849">This means when a user agent you've specified as exempt encounters an InfoPath form, the form will be returned as an XML file, instead of an entire web page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-850">这可以加速对 InfoPath 表单编制索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-850">This makes indexing InfoPath forms faster.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-851">更改了网络访问策略</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-851">Changed network access policy</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-852">NetworkAccessPolicyChanged</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-852">NetworkAccessPolicyChanged</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-853">SharePoint 或全局管理员在 SharePoint 管理中心或通过使用 SharePoint Online PowerShell 更改了基于位置的访问策略 (也称为 "受信任的网络边界")。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-853">A SharePoint or global administrator changed the location-based access policy (also called a trusted network boundary) in the SharePoint admin center or by using SharePoint Online PowerShell.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-854">此类型的策略控制谁可以根据您指定的授权 IP 地址范围访问组织中的 SharePoint 和 OneDrive 资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-854">This type of policy controls who can access SharePoint and OneDrive resources in your organization based on authorized IP address ranges that you specify.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-855">有关详细信息, 请参阅[基于网络位置控制对 SharePoint Online 和 OneDrive 数据的访问](https://support.office.com/article/b5a5f1f1-1174-4c6b-91d0-9273a6b6971f)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-855">For more information, see [Control access to SharePoint Online and OneDrive data based on network location](https://support.office.com/article/b5a5f1f1-1174-4c6b-91d0-9273a6b6971f).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-856">完成的网站地理位置移动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-856">Completed site geo move</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-857">SiteGeoMoveCompleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-857">SiteGeoMoveCompleted</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-858">组织中的全局管理员安排的网站地理位置移动已成功完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-858">A site geo move that was scheduled by a global administrator in your organization was successfully completed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-859">多地理位置功能可让 Office 365 组织跨多个 Office 365 数据中心地理位置, 这些地理位置称为信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-859">The Multi-Geo capability lets an Office 365 organization span multiple Office 365 datacenter geographies, which are called geos.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-860">有关详细信息, 请参阅[Office 365 中的 OneDrive 和 SharePoint Online 中的多地理位置功能](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-860">For more information, see [Multi-Geo Capabilities in OneDrive and SharePoint Online in Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=860840).</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-861">已创建发送到连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-861">Created Sent To connection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-862">SendToConnectionAdded</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-862">SendToConnectionAdded</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-863">SharePoint 或全局管理员在 SharePoint 管理中心的 "记录管理" 页上创建新的 "发送至" 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-863">A SharePoint or global administrator creates a new Send To connection on the Records management page in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-864">“发送至”连接指定文档存储库或记录中心设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-864">A Send To connection specifies settings for a document repository or a records center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-865">创建“发送至”连接时，内容管理器可以将文档提交到指定位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-865">When you create a Send To connection, a Content Organizer can submit documents to the specified location.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-866">创建的网站集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-866">Created site collection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-867">SiteCollectionCreated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-867">SiteCollectionCreated</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-868">SharePoint 或全局管理员在您的 SharePoint Online 组织中创建新的网站集, 或者用户预配其 OneDrive for business 网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-868">A SharePoint or global administrator creates a new site collection in your SharePoint Online organization or a user provisions their OneDrive for Business site.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-869">已删除孤立中心网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-869">Deleted orphaned hub site</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-870">HubSiteOrphanHubDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-870">HubSiteOrphanHubDeleted</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-871">SharePoint 或全局管理员删除了一个孤立的中心网站, 该站点是一个不具有任何与之关联的站点的中心网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-871">A SharePoint or global administrator deleted an orphan hub site, which is a hub site that doesn't have any sites associated with it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-872">孤立的集线器可能是由于删除了原始中心网站造成的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-872">An orphaned hub is likely caused by the deletion of the original hub site.</span></span> <br/>|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-873">删除已发送到连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-873">Deleted Sent To connection</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-874">SendToConnectionRemoved</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-874">SendToConnectionRemoved</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-875">SharePoint 或全局管理员在 SharePoint 管理中心的 "记录管理" 页上删除 "发送至" 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-875">A SharePoint or global administrator deletes a Send To connection on the Records management page in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-882">已启用旧版工作流</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-882">Enabled legacy workflow</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-883">LegacyWorkflowEnabledSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-883">LegacyWorkflowEnabledSet</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-884">网站管理员或所有者将 SharePoint 2013 工作流任务内容类型添加到网站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-884">Site administrator or owner adds the SharePoint 2013 Workflow Task content type to the site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-885">全局管理员还可以在 SharePoint 管理中心中启用整个组织的工作流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-885">Global administrators can also enable work flows for the entire organization in the SharePoint admin center.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-886">启用 Office on Demand</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-886">Enabled Office on Demand</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-887">OfficeOnDemandSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-887">OfficeOnDemandSet</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-888">网站管理员启用 Office on Demand，允许用户访问最新版本的 Office 桌面应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-888">Site administrator enables Office on Demand, which lets users access the latest version of Office desktop applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-889">SharePoint 管理中心启用了 Office on Demand，并需要包括全套已安装的 Office 应用程序的 Office 365 订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-889">Office on Demand is enabled in the SharePoint admin center and requires an Office 365 subscription that includes full, installed Office applications.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-890">人员搜索的已启用结果源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-890">Enabled result source for People Searches</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-891">PeopleResultsScopeSet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-891">PeopleResultsScopeSet</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-892">网站管理员为人员搜索网站的结果创建结果源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-892">Site administrator creates the result source for People Searches for a site.</span></span><br/>|

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-897">将网站加入中心网站</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-897">Joined site to hub site</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-898">HubSiteJoined</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-898">HubSiteJoined</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-899">网站所有者将其网站与中心网站相关联。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-899">A site owner associates their site with a hub site.</span></span><br/>|

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-904">删除了允许的数据位置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-904">Removed allowed data location</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-905">AllowedDataLocationDeleted</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-905">AllowedDataLocationDeleted</span></span><br/>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-906">SharePoint 或全局管理员在多地理位置环境中删除了允许的数据位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-906">A SharePoint or global administrator removed an allowed data location in a multi-geo environment.</span></span><br/>|

### <a name="exchange-mailbox-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-931">Exchange 邮箱活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-931">Exchange mailbox activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-932">下表列出了邮箱审核日志记录可以记录的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-932">The following table lists the activities that can be logged by mailbox audit logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-933">邮箱所有者、委派用户或管理员执行的邮箱活动将自动记录在最长90天的 Office 365 审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-933">Mailbox activities performed by the mailbox owner, a delegated user, or an administrator are automatically logged in the Office 365 audit log for up to 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-934">请注意, 管理员可以对 organizatin 中的所有用户关闭邮箱审核日志记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-934">Note that it's possible for an admin to turn off mailbox audit logging for all users in your organizatin.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-935">在这种情况下, 不会记录任何用户的邮箱操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-935">In this case, no mailbox actions for any user are are logged.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-936">有关详细信息, 请参阅[管理邮箱审核](enable-mailbox-auditing.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-936">For more information, see [Manage mailbox auditing](enable-mailbox-auditing.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="81889-937">您还可以使用 Exchange Online PowerShell 中的[search-mailboxauditlog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet 搜索邮箱活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-937">You can also search for mailbox activities by using the [Search-MailboxAuditLog](https://docs.microsoft.com/powershell/module/exchange/policy-and-compliance-audit/search-mailboxauditlog) cmdlet in Exchange Online PowerShell.</span></span> 
  
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-938">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-938">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-939">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-939">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-940">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-940">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-941">添加了委派邮箱权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-941">Added delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-942">AddMailboxPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-942">AddMailboxPermissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-943">管理员向其他人的邮箱分配了对用户 (称为代理) 的 FullAccess 邮箱权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-943">An administrator assigned the FullAccess mailbox permission to a user (known as a delegate) to another person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-944">FullAccess 权限允许代理打开其他人的邮箱, 并读取和管理邮箱的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-944">The FullAccess permission allows the delegate to open the other person's mailbox, and read and manage the contents of the mailbox.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-945">添加或删除了具有 "代理访问日历" 文件夹的用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-945">Added or removed user with delegate access to calendar folder</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-946">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-946">UpdateCalendarDelegation</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-947">将用户添加或删除为对其他用户邮箱的日历的代理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-947">A user was added or removed as a delegate to the calendar of another user's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-948">日历委派向同一组织中的其他人授予对邮箱所有者日历的管理权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-948">Calendar delegation gives someone else in the same organization permissions to manage the mailbox owner's calendar.</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-949">向文件夹添加了权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-949">Added permissions to folder</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-950">AddFolderPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-950">AddFolderPermissions</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-951">添加了一个文件夹权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-951">A folder permission was added.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-952">文件夹权限控制组织中的哪些用户可以访问邮箱中的文件夹和位于这些文件夹中的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-952">Folder permissions control which users in your organization can access folders in a mailbox and the messages located in those folders.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-953">将邮件复制到另一个文件夹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-953">Copied messages to another folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-954">Copy</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-954">Copy</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-955">已将某个邮件复制到另一个文件夹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-955">A message was copied to another folder.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-956">创建的邮箱项目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-956">Created mailbox item</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-957">Create</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-957">Create</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-958">在邮箱的日历、联系人、备注或任务文件夹中创建项目；例如，创建新的会议请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-958">An item is created in the Calendar, Contacts, Notes, or Tasks folder in the mailbox; for example, a new meeting request is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-959">请注意, 不会审核创建、发送或接收邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-959">Note that creating, sending, or receiving a message isn't audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-960">此外, 还不会审核创建邮箱文件夹的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-960">Also, creating a mailbox folder is not audited.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-961">在 Outlook web app 中创建了新的收件箱规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-961">Created new inbox rule in Outlook web app</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-962">NewInboxRule</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-962">NewInboxRule</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-963">邮箱所有者或对邮箱具有访问权限的其他用户在 Outlook web app 中创建了新的收件箱规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-963">A mailbox owner or other user with access to the mailbox created a new inbox rule in the Outlook web app.</span></span><br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-969">将邮件标记为记录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-969">Labeled message as a record</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-970">ApplyRecordLabel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-970">ApplyRecordLabel</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-971">邮件被分类为记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-971">A message was classified as a record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-972">当手动或自动应用将内容分类为记录时, 将发生这种情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-972">This occurs when a retention label that classifies content as a record is manually or automatically applied to a message.</span></span><br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-983">从 Outlook web app 修改的收件箱规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-983">Modified inbox rule from Outlook web app</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-984">SetInboxRule</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-984">SetInboxRule</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-985">邮箱所有者或对邮箱具有访问权限的其他用户使用 Outlook web app 修改了收件箱规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-985">A mailbox owner or other user with access to the mailbox modified an inbox rule using the Outlook web app.</span></span><br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-989">已删除委派邮箱权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-989">Removed delegate mailbox permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-990">Add-mailboxpermission</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-990">Remove-MailboxPermission</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-991">管理员从某人的邮箱中删除了 FullAccess 权限 (已分配给代理)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-991">An administrator removed the FullAccess permission (that was assigned to a delegate) from a person's mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-992">删除 FullAccess 权限后, 代理将无法打开其他人的邮箱或访问其中的任何内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-992">After the FullAccess permission is removed, the delegate can't open the other person's mailbox or access any content in it.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-993">从文件夹删除权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-993">Removed permissions from folder</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-994">RemoveFolderPermissions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-994">RemoveFolderPermissions</span></span><br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-995">已删除文件夹权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-995">A folder permission was removed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-996">文件夹权限控制组织中的哪些用户可以访问邮箱中的文件夹和位于这些文件夹中的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-996">Folder permissions control which users in your organization can access folders in a mailbox and the messages located in those folders.</span></span><br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-997">使用 "代理发送" 权限发送邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-997">Sent message using Send As permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-998">SendAs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-998">SendAs</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-999">邮件是使用 SendAs 权限发送的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-999">A message was sent using the SendAs permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1000">这表示另一个用户发送了邮件，而该邮件就好像来自于邮箱所有者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1000">This means another user sent the message as though it came from the mailbox owner.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="81889-1001">使用 "代表发送" 权限发送的邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1001">Sent message using Send On Behalf permissions</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-1002">SendOnBehalf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1002">SendOnBehalf</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-1003">邮件是使用 SendOnBehalf 权限发送的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1003">A message was sent using the SendOnBehalf permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1004">这表示另一个用户代表邮箱所有者发送了邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1004">This means another user sent the message on behalf of the mailbox owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1005">该邮件指示收件人代表发送邮件的收件人和实际发送邮件的收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1005">The message indicates to the recipient who the message was sent on behalf of and who actually sent the message.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-1009">更新的邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1009">Updated message</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-1010">Update</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1010">Update</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="81889-1011">更改了邮件或其属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1011">A message or its properties was changed.</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="azure-ad-group-administration-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1099">Azure AD 组管理活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1099">Azure AD group administration activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1100">下表列出了在管理员或用户创建或更改 Office 365 组时或者当管理员使用 Microsoft 365 管理中心或 Azure 管理门户创建安全组时记录的组管理活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1100">The following table lists group administration activities that are logged when an admin or a user creates or changes an Office 365 group or when an admin creates a security group by using the Microsoft 365 admin center or the Azure management portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1101">有关 Office 365 中的组的详细信息, 请参阅在[Microsoft 365 管理中心中查看、创建和删除组](https://support.office.com/article/a6360120-2fc4-46af-b105-6a04dc5461c7)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1101">For more information about groups in Office 365, see [View, create, and delete Groups in the Microsoft 365 admin center](https://support.office.com/article/a6360120-2fc4-46af-b105-6a04dc5461c7).</span></span>
