### <a name="ediscovery-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1208">电子数据展示活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1208">eDiscovery activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1209">在安全与合规中心中或通过运行相应的 PowerShell cmdlet 在审核日志中执行的内容搜索和电子数据展示相关的活动将记录在审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1209">Content Search and eDiscovery-related activities that are performed in the security and compliance center or by running the corresponding PowerShell cmdlets are logged in the audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1210">这包括以下活动:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1210">This includes the following activities:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1211">创建和管理电子数据展示事例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1211">Creating and managing eDiscovery cases</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1212">创建、启动和编辑内容搜索</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1212">Creating, starting, and editing Content Searches</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1213">执行内容搜索操作, 如预览、导出和删除搜索结果</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1213">Performing Content Search actions, such as previewing, exporting, and deleting search results</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1214">配置内容搜索的权限筛选</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1214">Configuring permissions filtering for Content Search</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1215">管理电子数据展示管理员角色</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1215">Managing the eDiscovery Administrator role</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1216">有关记录的电子数据展示活动的列表和详细说明, 请参阅[在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索电子数据展示活动](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1216">For a list and detailed description of the eDiscovery activities that are logged, see [Search for eDiscovery activities in the Office 365 audit log](search-for-ediscovery-activities-in-the-audit-log.md).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1217">在搜索结果中显示的 "**活动**" 下拉列表中的 "**电子数据展示活动**" 下列出的活动最长需要30分钟的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1217">It takes up to 30 minutes for events that result from the activities listed under **eDiscovery activities** in the **Activities** drop-down list to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1218">相反, 电子数据展示 cmdlet 活动中的相应事件需要长达24小时才会显示在搜索结果中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1218">Conversely, it takes up to 24 hours for the corresponding events from eDiscovery cmdlet activities to appear in the search results.</span></span>

### <a name="power-bi-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1299">Power BI 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1299">Power BI activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1300">可以在审核日志中搜索 Power BI 中的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1300">You can search the audit log for activities in Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1301">有关 Power BI 活动的信息, 请参阅在[组织中使用审核](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi)中的 "POWER power BI 审核的活动" 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1301">For information about Power BI activities, see the "Activities audited by Power Power BI" section in [Using auditing within your organization](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-auditing#activities-audited-by-power-bi).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1302">请注意, Power BI 的审核日志记录在默认情况下不启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1302">Note that audit logging for Power BI isn't enabled by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1303">若要在 Office 365 审核日志中搜索 Power BI 活动, 您必须在 Power BI 管理门户中启用审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1303">To search for Power BI activities in the Office 365 audit log, you have to enable auditing in the Power BI admin portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1304">有关说明, 请参阅[POWER BI 管理门户](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs)中的 "审核日志" 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1304">For instructions, see the "Audit logs" section in [Power BI admin portal](https://docs.microsoft.com/power-bi/service-admin-portal#audit-logs).</span></span>
  
### <a name="microsoft-workplace-analytics-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1305">Microsoft Workplace Analytics 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1305">Microsoft Workplace Analytics activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1306">工作区分析可深入了解如何在您的 Office 365 组织中进行组协作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1306">Workplace Analytics provides insight into how groups collaborate across your Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1307">下表列出了在工作区分析中分配了管理员角色或分析师角色的用户所执行的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1307">The following table lists activities performed by users that are assigned the Administrator role or the Analyst roles in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1308">分配了分析员角色的用户具有对所有服务功能的完全访问权限, 并使用产品进行分析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1308">Users assigned the Analyst role have full access to all service features and use the product to do analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1309">分配了管理员角色的用户可以配置隐私设置和系统默认设置, 并可以准备、上传和验证工作区分析中的组织数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1309">Users assigned the Administrator role can configure privacy settings and system defaults, and can prepare, upload, and verify organizational data in Workplace Analytics.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1310">有关详细信息, 请参阅[Workplace Analytics](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/workplace-analytics/index-orig)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1310">For more information, see [Workplace Analytics](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/workplace-analytics/index-orig).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="81889-1311">**易记名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1311">**Friendly name**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-1312">**操作**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1312">**Operation**</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="81889-1313">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1313">**Description**</span></span>|
|:-----|:-----|:-----|

### <a name="microsoft-teams-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1344">Microsoft 团队活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1344">Microsoft Teams activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1345">下表列出了 Microsoft 团队中记录的 Office 365 审核日志中的用户和管理员活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1345">The following table lists the user and admin activities in Microsoft Teams that are logged in the Office 365 audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1346">Microsoft 团队是 Office 365 中一个聊天中心的工作区。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1346">Microsoft Teams is a chat-centered workspace in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1347">它将团队的对话、会议、文件和笔记集中在一个位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1347">It brings a team's conversations, meetings, files and notes together into a single place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1348">有关详细信息和指向帮助主题的链接, 请参阅:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1348">For more information and links to help topics, see:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="81889-1349">有关 Microsoft 团队的常见问题-管理员帮助</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1349">Frequently asked questions about Microsoft Teams - Admin Help</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/05cbe533-2181-4e95-a4b0-52cd7695fafc)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="81889-1350">Microsoft 团队帮助</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1350">Microsoft Teams help</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/23156c0c-2c6e-49dd-8b7b-7c564b76508c)

owner.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1408">对于这些活动中的每个活动, 在审核日志搜索结果的 "**项目**" 列中显示了已更改的设置 (如下面的括号中所示) 的说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1408">For each of these data-ttu-id="81889-1409">-更改团队的访问类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1409">- Changes the access type for a team.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1410">可以将团队设置为私有或公共 (**团队访问类型**)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1410">Teams can be set as Private or Public ( **Team access type**).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1411">当团队为私有时 (默认设置), 用户只能通过邀请访问团队。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1411">When a team is private (the default setting), users can access the team only by invitation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1412">如果团队是公共的, 则任何人都能发现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1412">When a team is public, it's discoverable by anyone.</span></span>  <br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="81889-1413">-更改团队的信息分类 (**团队分类**)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1413">- Changes the information classification of a team ( **Team classification**).</span></span>  <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-1414">例如, 可以将团队数据分类为业务影响高、业务影响或业务影响较低。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1414">For example, team data can be classified as high business impact, medium business impact, or low business impact.</span></span><br/><br/><span data-ttu-id="81889-1415">-更改团队的名称 (**团队名称**)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1417">- Changes made to any of the team settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1418">团队所有者可以通过右键单击团队, 单击 "**管理团队**", 然后单击 "**设置**" 选项卡来访问团队客户端中的这些设置。对于这些活动, ### <a name="microsoft-flow-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1514">Microsoft 流活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1514">Microsoft Flow activities</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1515">可以在审核日志中搜索 Microsoft Flow 中的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1515">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Flow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1516">这些活动包括创建、编辑和删除流以及更改流权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1516">These activities include creating, editing and deleting flows, and changing flow permissions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1517">有关流活动审核的信息, 请参阅现已[在安全 & 合规中心中提供的博客 Microsoft 流审核事件](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/security-and-compliance-center)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1517">For information about auditing for Flow activities, see the blog  [Microsoft Flow audit events now available in Security & Compliance Center](https://flow.microsoft.com/blog/security-and-compliance-center).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-powerapps"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1518">Microsoft PowerApps</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1518">Microsoft PowerApps</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1519">您可以在 PowerApps 中搜索与应用程序相关的活动的审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1519">You can search the audit log for app-related activities in PowerApps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1520">这些活动包括创建、启动和发布应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1520">These activities include creating, launching, and publishing an app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1521">还会审核对应用程序分配权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1521">Assigning permissions to apps is also audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1522">有关所有 PowerApps 活动的说明, 请参阅[powerapps 的活动日志记录](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/power-platform/admin/logging-powerapps#what-events-are-audited)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1522">For a description of all PowerApps activities, see [Activity logging for PowerApps](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/power-platform/admin/logging-powerapps#what-events-are-audited).</span></span>

### <a name="microsoft-stream-activities"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1523">Microsoft Stream 活动</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1523">Microsoft Stream activities</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1524">可以在审核日志中搜索 Microsoft Stream 中的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1524">You can search the audit log for activities in Microsoft Stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1525">这些活动包括用户执行的视频活动、组频道活动和管理活动, 如管理用户、管理组织设置和导出报告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1525">These activities include video activities performed by users, group channel activities, and admin activities such as managing users, managing organization settings, and exporting reports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1526">有关这些活动的说明, 请参阅[Microsoft stream 中的审核日志](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs)中的 "microsoft stream 中记录的活动" 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1526">For a description of these activities, see the "Activities logged in Microsoft Stream" section in [Audit Logs in Microsoft Stream](https://docs.microsoft.com/stream/audit-logs).</span></span>

### <a name="exchange-admin-audit-log"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1527">Exchange 管理员审核日志</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1527">Exchange admin audit log</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1528">Exchange 管理员审核日志记录 (默认情况下在 Office 365 中启用) 在管理员 (或已分配管理权限的用户) 在 Exchange Online 组织中进行更改时, 会在 Office 365 审核日志中记录一个事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1528">Exchange administrator audit logging—which is enabled by default in Office 365—logs an event in the Office 365 audit log when an administrator (or a user who has been assigned administrative permissions) makes a change in your Exchange Online organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1529">通过使用 Exchange 管理中心或通过在 Windows PowerShell 中运行 cmdlet 所做的更改将记录在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1529">Changes made by using the Exchange admin center or by running a cmdlet in Windows PowerShell are logged in the Exchange admin audit log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1530">有关 Exchange 中的管理员审核日志记录的更多详细信息, 请参阅[管理员审核日志记录](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1530">For more detailed information about admin audit logging in Exchange, see [Administrator audit logging](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=619225).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1531">以下是在 Exchange 管理员审核日志中搜索活动的一些提示:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1531">Here are some tips for searching for activity in the Exchange admin audit log:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1532">若要从 Exchange 管理员审核日志中返回条目, 您必须在 "**活动**" 列表中选择 "**显示所有活动的结果**"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1532">To return entries from the Exchange admin audit log, you have to select **Show results for all activities** in the **Activities** list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1533">使用 "日期范围" 框和 "**用户**" 列表可缩小特定日期范围内特定 Exchange 管理员运行的 cmdlet 的搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1533">Use the date range boxes and the **Users** list to narrow the search results for cmdlets run by a specific Exchange administrator within a specific date range.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1534">若要显示来自 Exchange 管理员审核日志的事件, 请筛选搜索结果并在**-** "**活动**筛选器" 框中键入 a (划线)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1534">To display events from the Exchange admin audit log, filter the search results and type a **-** (dash) in the **Activity** filter box.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1535">这将显示在 Exchange 管理员事件的 "**活动**" 列中显示的 cmdlet 名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1535">This will display cmdlet names, which are displayed in the **Activity** column for Exchange admin events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1536">然后, 您可以按字母顺序对 cmdlet 名称进行排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1536">Then you can sort the cmdlet names in alphabetical order.</span></span> 
    
    ![在 "活动" 框中键入一个短划线以筛选 Exchange 管理员事件](media/7628e7aa-6263-474a-a28b-2dcf5694bb27.png)
  
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1538">若要获取有关运行什么 cmdlet、使用的参数和参数值以及受影响的对象的信息, 您必须导出搜索结果并选择 "**下载所有结果**" 选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1538">To get information about what cmdlet was run, which parameters and parameter values were used, and what objects were affected, you will have to export the search results and select the **Download all results** option.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1539">您还可以使用 Exchange 管理中心查看 Exchange 管理员审核日志中的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1539">You can also view events in the Exchange admin audit log by using the Exchange admin center.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1540">有关说明, 请参阅[查看管理员审核日志](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/dn342832%28v=exchg.150%29.aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1540">For instructions, see [View the administrator audit log](https://technet.microsoft.com/library/dn342832%28v=exchg.150%29.aspx).</span></span>
  
## <a name="frequently-asked-questions"></a><span data-ttu-id="81889-1541">常见问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1541">Frequently asked questions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1542">**在哪里可以找到由 Office 365 中的审计服务提供的功能？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1542">**Where can I find about the features offered by the auditing service in Office 365?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1543">有关 Office 365 中提供的审核和报告功能的详细信息, 请参阅[office 365 中的审核和报告](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1543">For more information about the auditing and reporting features available in Office 365, see [Auditing and Reporting in Office 365](office-365-auditing-and-reporting-overview.md).</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1544">**目前已审核的 Office 365 服务有什么不同？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1544">**What are different Office 365 services that are currently audited?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1545">审核最常用的 Office 365 服务, 如 Exchange Online、SharePoint Online、OneDrive for Business、Azure Active Directory、Microsoft 团队、Dynamics 365、高级威胁防护和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1545">The most used Office 365 services like Exchange Online, SharePoint Online, OneDrive for Business, Azure Active Directory, Microsoft Teams, Dynamics 365, Advanced Threat Protection, and Power BI are audited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1546">若要审核的服务列表, 请参阅[本文的开头部分](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1546">See the [beginning of this article](search-the-audit-log-in-security-and-compliance.md) for a list of services that are audited.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1547">**哪些活动由 Office 365 中的审核服务进行审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1547">**What activities are audited by auditing service in Office 365?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1548">请参阅本文中的 "[审核的活动](#audited-activities)" 一节, 以获取 Office 365 中审核的活动的列表和说明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1548">See the [Audited activities](#audited-activities) section in this article for a list and description of the activities that are audited in Office 365.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1549">**在事件发生后, 审核记录需要多长时间才能使用？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1549">**How long does it take for an auditing record to be available after an event has occurred?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1550">大多数审核数据在30分钟内可用, 但在事件发生后, 可能需要长达24小时才能在搜索结果中显示相应的审核日志条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1550">Most auditing data is available within 30 minutes but it may take up to 24 hours after an event occurs for the corresponding audit log entry to be displayed in the search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1551">请参阅本文的 "[开始之前](#before-you-begin)" 一节中的表, 其中显示了不同 Office 365 服务中的事件所需的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1551">See the table in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section of this article that shows the time it takes for events in the different Office 365 services to be available.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1552">**审核记录保留多长时间？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1552">**How long are the audit records retained for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1553">正如前面所述, 审核记录的保留期取决于组织的 Office 365 订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1553">As previously explained, the retention period for audit records depends on your organization's Office 365 subscription.</span></span>  

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1554">**Office 365 E3** -审核记录保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1554">**Office 365 E3** - Audit records are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="81889-1555">**Office 365 E5** -审核记录也会保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1555">**Office 365 E5** - Audit records are also retained for 90 days.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1556">保留一年的审核记录可能最终适用于拥有 E3 许可证和 Office 365 高级合规性附加许可证的 E5 用户和用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1556">Retaining audit records for one year may eventually be available for E5 users and users with an E3 license and an Office 365 Advanced Compliance add-on license.</span></span>

     > [!NOTE]
     > <span data-ttu-id="81889-1557">如前所述, 针对 E5 组织的审核记录的为期一年的专用预览计划 (或具有高级合规性附加许可证的 E3 组织) 已关闭到新的注册。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1557">As previously explained, the private preview program for the one-year retention period for audit records for E5 organizations (or E3 organizations that have Advanced Compliance add-on licenses) is closed to new enrollment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1558">此文章将在公开预览版中的一年保留期可用或发布以用于正式可用性时进行更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1558">This article will be updated when the one-year retention period is available in public preview or released for general availability.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1559">另请注意, 审核记录的保留期的持续时间基于每用户许可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1559">Also note that the duration of the retention period for audit records is based on per-user licensing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1560">例如, 如果为组织中的某个用户分配了 Office 365 E3 或 E5 许可证, 则该用户执行的活动的审核记录将保留90天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1560">For example, if a user in your organization is assigned an Office 365 E3 or E5 license, then the audit records for activities performed by that user are retained for 90 days.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1561">**我是否可以以编程方式访问审核数据？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1561">**Can I access the auditing data programmatically?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1562">是。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1562">Yes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1563">Office 365 管理活动 API 用于以编程方式提取审核日志。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1563">The Office 365 Management Activity API is used to fetch the audit logs programmatically.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="81889-1564">若要开始, 请参阅[Office 365 管理 api](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis)入门。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1564">To get started, see [Get started with Office 365 Management APIs](https://docs.microsoft.com/office/office-365-management-api/get-started-with-office-365-management-apis).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1565">**是否有其他方法可以获取除使用安全和合规中心或 Office 365 管理活动 API 之外的审核日志？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1565">**Are there other ways to get auditing logs other than using the security and compliance center or the Office 365 Management Activity API?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1566">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1566">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1567">下面是从 Office 365 审核服务中获取数据的两种方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1567">These are the only two ways to get data from the Office 365 auditing service.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1568">**我是否需要在每个要为其捕获审核日志的服务中单独启用审核？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1568">**Do I need to individually enable auditing in each service that I want to capture audit logs for?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1569">在大多数 Office 365 服务中, 在您最初为 Office 365 组织启用审核 (如本文的 "[开始之前](#before-you-begin)" 一节中所述) 后, 默认情况下将启用审核功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1569">In most Office 365 services, auditing is enabled by default after you initially turn on auditing for your Office 365 organization (as described in the [Before you begin](#before-you-begin) section in this article).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1570">但是, 您必须为要审核的每个邮箱在 Exchange Online 中启用邮箱审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1570">However, you have to enable mailbox auditing in Exchange Online for each mailbox that you want to audit.</span></span>   <span data-ttu-id="81889-1571">我们正在努力为 Office 365 组织中的所有邮箱默认启用邮箱审核。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1571">We are working on enabling mailbox auditing by default for all mailboxes in an Office 365 organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1572">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Microsoft 安全性、隐私与合规性博客](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Security-Privacy-and-Compliance/Exchange-Mailbox-Auditing-will-be-enabled-by-default/ba-p/215171)中的“Exchange 邮箱审核将默认处于启用状态”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1572">For more information, see "Exchange mailbox auditing will be enabled by default" in the [Microsoft Security, Privacy, and Compliance blog](https://techcommunity.microsoft.com/t5/Security-Privacy-and-Compliance/Exchange-Mailbox-Auditing-will-be-enabled-by-default/ba-p/215171).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1573">**Office 365 审核服务是否支持对记录进行重复数据消除？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1573">**Does the Office 365 auditing service support de-duplication of records?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1574">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1574">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1575">审核服务管道接近实时, 因此无法支持重复数据消除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1575">The auditing service pipeline is near real time, and therefore can't support de-duplication.</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1576">**Office 365 是否跨地理位置审核数据流？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1576">**Does Office 365 auditing data flow across geographies?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1577">否。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1577">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1578">我们目前在 NA (北美)、EMEA (欧洲、中东和非洲) 和 APAC (亚太地区) 区域中审核管道部署。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1578">We currently have auditing pipeline deployments in the NA (North America), EMEA (Europe, Middle east and Africa) and APAC (Asia Pacific) regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1579">但是, 我们可能会在这些区域之间传输数据以进行负载平衡, 并且仅在实时站点问题中流动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1579">However, we may flow the data across these regions for load-balancing and only during live-site issues.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1580">当我们执行这些活动时, 将对传输中的数据进行加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1580">When we do perform these activities, the data in transit is encrypted.</span></span>   
 
<span data-ttu-id="81889-1581">**审核数据是否已加密？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1581">**Is auditing data encrypted?**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="81889-1582">审核数据存储在部署审核管道的同一区域中的 Exchange 邮箱 (静态数据) 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1582">Auditing data is stored in Exchange mailboxes (data at rest) in the same region where the auditing pipeline is deployed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1583">此数据不加密。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1583">This data is not encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="81889-1584">但是, 传输中的数据总是加密的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81889-1584">However, data in transit is always encrypted.</span></span>
